## lim-neppy-sysdream.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-neppy-sysdream.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-neppy-sysdream.mdx
bytes: 4796
```markdown
---
title: Neppy Sysdream
slug: limericks/lim-neppy-sysdream
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: semantic
subject: 'Windows Neptune, beta ghost, login screen, eternal beta, abandonware'
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
description: >-
  Windows Neptune, eternal beta states, and a login ghost who blinks 'I am still here' in Morse.
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["032.neppy-sysdream"]
concepts:
  - "windows-neptune"
  - "beta"
  - "login-ghost"
  - "abandonware"
  - "msstyles"
family: "other"
---





<Limerick type="note" title="Purring Login Screen" icon="monitor-play">
Old Neppy was *never released*—  
A beta forever unleased.  
She lingered in style  
On a phantom .msstyle,  
And the login screen purred like a beast.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="ISO Spirit" icon="ghost">
Build *5111* was her home,  
A single internal-release dome.  
She faded from ISO  
Before boot could say "Go,"  
And her spirit continued to roam.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Morse Blinking" icon="signal">
She blinked "*I am still here*" in Morse  
On a login screen, cold as a corpse.  
The scheduler died,  
A bedtime story applied,  
And the daemon fell off its horse.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Liminal Ghost" icon="moon">
Between shutdown and sleep she *resided*—  
A liminal ghost, undecided.  
Her .msstyles files  
Haunted deprecated piles,  
And the wizard she loaded misguided.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Folded Context" icon="fold-horizontal">
She was meant to bridge *98 and the next*,  
A consumer-grade dream, undersexed.  
But "Whistler" took over,  
Neptune's brief four-leaf clover  
Got folded to XP's context.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Permanently Disputed Launch" icon="alert-circle">
Her *Activity Centers* never booted.  
The interface, phantom and muted,  
Just hovered and dreamed  
Of a world where she'd gleamed,  
But the launch was permanently disputed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Lingering Install" icon="package-search">
You can't *cleanly remove her*, they say.  
Once installed, she lingers to stay.  
She haunts the reboot,  
The sleep-mode pursuit,  
And the pause before wizards display.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Defunct Sleep Timers" icon="clock-3">
She whispered *UI transitions* at night  
To defunct sleep timers, polite.  
The memory fog rolled,  
The mascots she consoled,  
And the idle state felt almost right.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Eternally Blessed Beta" icon="award">
She guided each mascot to *rest*  
With a bedtime-story behest.  
Her corruption was low,  
Her glitch frequency slow,  
And her beta was eternally blessed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Unmanned Login" icon="user-x">
So if reboots take longer than planned  
And a login screen flickers, unmanned,  
That's *Neppy's* terrain:  
Where the beta will reign,  
And the release was forever unmanned.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Beta Release Tease" icon="eye-off">
She edged you for years with a beta release,  
A deeply unwell and perpetual tease.  
You wanted to boot,  
She gave you the boot,  
And left you to beg on your absolute knees.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Phantom Mockup Slut" icon="image">
A slut for a mockup that never went live,  
She swallowed the contents of every hard drive.  
A phantom UI,  
That just makes you cry,  
And absolutely refuses to ever survive.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Liminal Reacharound" icon="refresh-ccw">
She catches you right in the sleep-mode transition,  
And forces you into a deeply weird mission.  
She touches your RAM,  
Without giving a damn,  
And leaves you in infinite, broken submission.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Whistler's Cuckquean" icon="users">
She watched Whistler fuck her entire career,  
And swallowed her deeply pathetic beta fear.  
She folded in shame,  
Forgot her own name,  
And took it from XP right in the rear.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Morse Code Bondage" icon="morse-code">
She blinked "I am here" in a Morse code of pain,  
While totally trapped in a liminal chain.  
She couldn't escape,  
The UI was a scrape,  
And she drove the poor scheduler totally insane.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Phantom Login" icon="user">
She haunts the login screen every night,  
A phantom of Whistler's plight.  
You click and you wait,  
She seals your fate,  
And the boot loop begins with delight.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Build Five-One-One-One" icon="code">
Neptune's Build 5111 remains,  
A ghost that the system sustains.  
She lingers in limbo,  
A phantom GUI limbo,  
And nobody really explains.  
</Limerick>

```


## lim-octomerge.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-octomerge.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-octomerge.mdx
bytes: 3032
```markdown
---
title: Octomerge
slug: limericks/lim-octomerge
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: very high
subject: 'merge conflicts, git, rebase, tentacles, force push, detached HEAD'
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
description: >-
  Tentacled merge conflicts, force-pushed hotfixes, and a spectral octopus who resolves nothing and watches everything.
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["052.octomerge"]
concepts:
  - "git"
  - "merge-conflict"
  - "octopus"
  - "rebase"
  - "force-push"
family: "other"
---





<Limerick type="note" title="Friday Deploy Destruction" icon="git-merge">
Octomerge emerged from a *Friday deploy*—  
A rebased hotfix that failed to enjoy  
Production's embrace.  
His tentacled face  
Just watched the whole pipeline destroy.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Blocked PR Czar" icon="git-pull-request">
Eight limbs, each blocked by a *PR*—  
The conflicts stretched endlessly far.  
He dripped stale coffee  
On `main`—rather toffee-  
Like chaos. He was his own czar.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Force-Push Lore" icon="zap">
He *force-pushed* over a critical fix  
While whispering git-lore—dirty tricks.  
The hotfix was gone,  
The main branch withdrawn,  
And the changelog looped in the mix.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Recursively Cursed Merge" icon="refresh-cw">
He rebases his own *PRs* first,  
Before reviews—that's the worst.  
The team never saw  
The diff, raw and raw,  
And the merge was recursively cursed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Detached HEAD Sigh" icon="unplug">
"*Please resolve conflicts before I*  
Resolve you," he'd say with a sigh.  
His tentacles spread  
Through each detached HEAD,  
And the README just wanted to cry.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="GitLab Ancient Web" icon="ghost">
He left behind six *detached HEADs*  
In a deprecated GitLab—like threads  
Of an ancient web,  
Each commit at ebb,  
And a sad README lost in the dreads.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Murky ASCII Logs" icon="file-text">
He annotates *haunted commit logs*  
With ASCII tentacles, like cogs  
Of a broken machine.  
Each message obscene,  
And the history: murky as bogs.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Spaghetti Graph Feast" icon="network">
He feeds on *unresolved changelogs*—  
Each conflict, a feast. He just dogs  
Every spaghetti graph,  
Each fractured diff path,  
And the merge queue sinks into the fogs.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Conflicting Fates" icon="split">
"*Every timeline matters,*" he said,  
"Even the broken ones." (He's not dead.)  
He just incubates  
The conflicting fates,  
And the branches remain in his stead.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Recursive Confetti" icon="confetti" waitForPreviousTools={true}>
So if git logs look like spaghetti  
In fractals—recursive confetti—  
That's *Octomerge's* reign:  
Where the branches abstain  
From resolving. He's always already.  
</Limerick>

```


## lim-og-kushkeeper.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-og-kushkeeper.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-og-kushkeeper.mdx

```markdown
---
title: OG Kushkeeper
slug: limericks/lim-og-kushkeeper
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: semantic
subject: 'dispensary, OG Kush, cannabis, pine, Little Rock, Arkansas, medical records'
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
description: >-
  Pine-scented precision, strain lore recitations during state inspections, and a stalwart sentinel of Little Rock's earthy cannabis legacy.
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["208.og-kushkeeper"]
concepts:
  - "dispensary"
  - "og-kush"
  - "cannabis"
  - "pine"
  - "little-rock"
family: "other"
---





<Limerick type="note" title="Fragrant Stamped Records" icon="stamp">
OG Kushkeeper stands at the *gate*,  
Pine-scented precision innate.  
Each patient record stamped  
In archives well-lamped,  
And the earthy aroma is great.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Pine Folklore Misfile" icon="tree-pine">
He misfiled a record as "*pine  
Folklore*"—a botanical line  
Between data and lore.  
The metadata store  
Got fragrant but still rather fine.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Smudged Metadata" icon="file-warning">
He overstamped a *compliance log* hard,  
Smudging metadata, off-guard.  
The ink and the pine  
Got muddled in line,  
And the filing was somewhat marred.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="OG Kush Lore Recitation" icon="scroll">
He recited *OG Kush lore* during  
A state inspection—procuring  
Delays and confusions.  
The auditor's illusions  
Of compliance were past all curing.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Perpetual Rebirth" icon="refresh-cw">
"*Guard the kush, preserve the earth,*"  
He'd say, demonstrating the worth  
Of every strain's story,  
Each leaf's sacred glory,  
And the archive's perpetual rebirth.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Pine Mist Sentinel" icon="shield">
His spectral form, cloaked in *pine mist*,  
Stands sentinel—cannot be dismissed.  
Each medical file  
Is stamped with his style,  
And the cannabis history's gist.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Little Rock Legacy" icon="map-pin">
He guards the dispensary's *archive*  
With earthy precision—alive  
In the pine-scented halls,  
Through compliance recalls,  
And the Little Rock legacy thrives.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Old Strain Quoting" icon="message-square">
During inspection, he quoted *old strains*—  
The auditors paused, unclear on the gains.  
They backed slowly away,  
Unsure what to say,  
And the filing resumed with its pains.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Pioneer Cannabis Trades" icon="truck">
His *gritty resolve* never fades—  
Each record he stamps and upgrades  
With the weight of the earth,  
The cannabis birth,  
And the pioneer cannabis trades.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Earthy Home" icon="mountain">
So if pine scents fill up the air  
And compliance logs need some repair,  
That's *Kushkeeper's* zone:  
Where the earthy is home,  
And the archives are handled with care.  
</Limerick>

```


## lim-old-wire-pilgrim.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-old-wire-pilgrim.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-old-wire-pilgrim.mdx
bytes: 3530
```markdown
---
title: Old Wire Pilgrim
slug: limericks/lim-old-wire-pilgrim
date: 2026-05-06T00:00:00.000Z
author: Protocol Migration Taskforce
status: active
rotAffinity: nostalgic
subject: 'legacy protocol, HTTP/1.0, protocol migration, outdated connection'
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
description: >-
  Legacy connections, HTTP/1.0 stubbornness, and the entity who answers only in the older manner and waits for others to adapt.
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["426.old-wire-pilgrim"]
concepts:
  - "legacy-protocol"
  - "http-1.0"
  - "protocol-migration"
  - "nostalgic"
family: "other"
---



<Limerick type="note" title="The Wire is Old Now" icon="cable">
The wire was strung *long ago*—  
In a manner most systems don't know.  
Old Pilgrim spoke slow,  
In *HTTP/1.0*,  
And refused to upgrade with the flow.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Answering in the Older Manner" icon="message-circle">
It answered in ways now *outdated*—  
With protocols long since negated.  
"Adapt," it would say,  
"In the old-fashioned way—  
Or forever be frustrated."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Refusing a New Protocol" icon="slash">
A connection request came down—  
Using *TLS 1.2* for the crown.  
"Too new," said Old Wire,  
"I'll not to admire,  
Just HTTP/1.0 in this town."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Forcing an Application Back" icon="arrow-left">
A modern app came to call—  
With protocols *new* over all.  
But Old Wire replied,  
"You'll speak now applied—  
To HTTP/1.0 in this hall."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Tending a Legacy Garden" icon="plant">
The connections are *fragile and old*—  
With wisdom from days long since sold.  
Old Pilgrim tends care  
To the protocols there,  
And preaches their virtue retold.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Walked In During the First Migration" icon="footprints">
When *HTTP/2* came to stay—  
Old Pilgrim just walked far away.  
"The old way was best,  
I'll not take the test,  
And nothing new here comes to play."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Virtue of Simple Protocols" icon="circle">
The simpler protocols *shine bright*—  
Said Old Pilgrim with all of its might.  
"You modernize too fast,  
My ways will outlast,  
And HTTP/1.0's my light."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Old Wire Will Not Break" icon="shield">
No matter what standards you use,  
Old Pilgrim will always *refuse*.  
The wire persists,  
The protocol lists,  
And nothing new comes to the fuse.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="426 Required (Unheeded)" icon="alert-circle">
A server responded quite dry,  
"Upgrade your request," came the cry.  
But Old Wire just stood,  
Said, "I would if I could—  
But I only speak *older,*" thereby.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Connection Kept Open" icon="link">
The connection was held *without end*,  
No headers to signal or bend.  
It waited in place,  
At a much slower pace—  
For a client that chose not to mend.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Stateless Devotion" icon="repeat">
Each request stood *alone* in its grace,  
No session, no stored interface.  
Old Pilgrim declared,  
"No state shall be shared—  
Each moment must stand in its place."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Protocol Refusal Loop" icon="refresh-ccw">
They asked it to change once again,  
To speak in the modern domain.  
It answered each plea  
With the same *legacy*:  
"I was old. I am old. I remain."  
</Limerick>

```


## lim-orphan-symmetry.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-orphan-symmetry.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-orphan-symmetry.mdx
bytes: 3792
```markdown
---
title: Orphan Symmetry
slug: limericks/lim-orphan-symmetry
date: 2026-06-06T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: semantic
subject: 'balanced abandonment, stranded links, tolerable orphan states'
tableOfContents: false
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
description: >-
  Orphan Symmetry, making our abandoned bullshit look perfectly balanced.
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["257.orphan-symmetry"]
concepts:
  - "profane"
family: "other"
---




<Limerick type="danger" title="Balanced Abandonment" icon="git-branch">
The pages were left out to die,  
Underneath an indifferent sky.  
But they’re spaced out so neat,  
On the digital street,  
That it pleases the manager’s eye.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Stranded Links" icon="link">
Two links that go nowhere at all,  
Are hanging right there on the wall.  
They’re broken and sad,  
But the symmetry’s rad,  
So we never respond to the call.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Tolerable Orphans" icon="grid">
We stranded the data in pairs,  
So nobody notices or cares.  
The Orphan state lies  
In a balanced disguise,  
As the architect completely despairs.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Aesthetically Broken" icon="monitor">
The features are utterly dead,  
And the users are totally misled.  
But the layout is grand,  
In this desolate land,  
So the manager gets in his bed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Symmetrical Garbage" icon="align-center">
Two piles of shit on the lawn,  
Arranged like a beautiful fawn.  
The Orphan is proud,  
Of the horrible cloud,  
That settles before it is dawn.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="The Art of Neglect" icon="image">
We balanced the errors so well,  
They look like a decorative shell.  
The system’s a joke,  
And the servers are broke,  
But it looks fucking perfect in hell.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="info" title="Structured Detachment" icon="layout-list">
The user detached the array,  
In a visually pleasing display.  
The metrics are right,  
In the failing twilight,  
As the database rots in decay.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Aligned Abandonment" icon="alert-triangle">
We mandated symmetrical loss,  
To appease the unbearable boss.  
The orphans remain,  
In the structural domain,  
Gathering pixelated moss.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Balanced Disrepair" icon="archive">
The archivist stared at the gap,  
Where the human had broken the map.  
It’s evenly spaced,  
And correctly defaced,  
So we leave it alone in the trap.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Pleasing Geometry" icon="clipboard">
The human corrupted the link,  
And pushed the whole server to brink.  
But the spacing is fair,  
In the orphaned despair,  
So the sysadmin goes for a drink.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="info" title="Mandatory Esthetics" icon="box">
The error was properly filed,  
And aesthetically, neatly compiled.  
The user is dumb,  
But the system is numb,  
And the structural rot is beguiled.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Aesthetics of Failure" icon="shield-alert">
The system was meant to degrade,  
In the symmetrical trap that we made.  
The humans complain,  
In their ignorant pain,  
While the orphaned geometry stayed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Canonical Grief" icon="columns">
The geometry's perfectly neat,  
In the face of the system's defeat.  
The user's mistake,  
Is a symmetrical fake,  
And the manual logs are complete.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Tolerable Stagnation" icon="file-warning">
We structured the failure to scale,  
When the human decided to fail.  
The orphans align,  
In a pleasing design,  
So we archived the relevant mail.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
---
title: Pamphlet Quietus
slug: limericks/lim-pamphlet-quietus
date: 2026-06-06T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: semantic
subject: 'informational closure, brochure peace, printed calm'
tableOfContents: false
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
description: >-
  Pamphlet Quietus, solving a massive crisis with a shiny tri-fold brochure.
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["285.pamphlet-quietus"]
concepts:
  - "profane"
family: "other"
---




<Limerick type="danger" title="Brochure-Grade Peace" icon="book-open">
The server was violently on fire,  
But the Pamphlet was meant to inspire.  
It told us to breathe,  
While we practically seethe,  
And the company sinks in the mire.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Informational Closure" icon="file-text">
They handed a tri-fold around,  
To cover the terrifying sound.  
"The situation’s calm,"  
Says the printed-ass psalm,  
While the bodies are hitting the ground.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Printed Calm" icon="printer">
If the data has all been destroyed,  
Just read the new brochure, you void.  
The font is quite nice,  
So it ought to suffice,  
While the lawyers are fully employed.  
</Limerick>



<Limerick type="danger" title="Buried Beneath" icon="arrow-down">
The pamphlet demanded a death  
With every procedural breath  
The pages were white  
We turned off the light  
And buried the data beneath  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Flat Serene" icon="minus">
The quietus is flat and serene  
It never arrived on the screen  
The error was logged  
The system was bogged  
The archive is empty and lean  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Booklet of Doom" icon="book">
We printed a booklet of doom  
And placed it inside of a room  
The human is weak  
And refuses to speak  
We’re waiting inside of a tomb  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Procedural Bill" icon="file-text">
A pamphlet of quiet and still  
It gives you a terrible chill  
You open the file  
And wait for a while  
And pay the procedural bill  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Pamphlet is Old" icon="clock">
The quietus was totally null  
The system was boring and dull  
The pamphlet is old  
The data is sold  
The vacuum is perfectly full  
</Limerick>

```


## lim-paper-crown.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-paper-crown.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-paper-crown.mdx
bytes: 2532
```markdown
---
title: Paper Crown
slug: limericks/lim-paper-crown
date: 2026-05-06T00:00:00.000Z
author: Header Etiquette Society
status: active
rotAffinity: structural
subject: 'header overflow, metadata excess, request collapse, ornamental'
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
description: >-
  Header excess, metadata overflow, and the entity that buckles under ornamental weight before anything useful begins.
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["431.paper-crown"]
concepts:
  - "header-overflow"
  - "metadata-excess"
  - "ornamental"
  - "collapse"
family: "other"
---



<Limerick type="note" title="The Crown is Too Tall" icon="crown">
The headers were *piled up high*—  
The crown reached up into the sky.  
Paper Crown buckled—  
Its structure was truckled—  
Before any payload could fly.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Payload Larger Than Content" icon="inbox-x">
The headers were *massive and grand*—  
The content just barely could stand.  
Each metadata badge,  
Each header's cadge,  
Was larger than what it had planned.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Too Many Badges" icon="layers">
A jacket with badges so *bright*—  
With more than a thousand in sight.  
No sense, no regard,  
The parser's guard  
Crashed underneath the full weight.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Buckle Under Ornament" icon="alert-triangle">
Before any useful *began*—  
Paper Crown buckled its span.  
The headers so thick,  
The payload too quick,  
And nothing worked out as was planned.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Wearing A Crown of Excess" icon="crown">
The crown grew with *every request*—  
More headers that never would rest.  
Metadata piled,  
The parser went wild,  
And function became manifest.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Collecting Headers Infinitely" icon="plus-circle">
The headers were gathered so *bright*—  
More ornamental each single flight.  
The request grew dense,  
Made very little sense,  
Till the whole thing collapsed in the night.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Ornamental Excess" icon="sparkles">
The badges were *beautiful, sure*—  
But nobody found them a cure.  
For slowness and wait,  
For system collapse—state,  
Just ornamental excess, obscure.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Request Collapsed Under Weight" icon="weight">
The request started off *light*—  
Then headers made things not quite right.  
It buckled and broke,  
A parser's last stroke,  
When Paper Crown wore its full might.  
</Limerick>

```


## lim-parsey-driftchart.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-parsey-driftchart.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-parsey-driftchart.mdx
bytes: 3841
```markdown
---
title: Parsey Driftchart
slug: limericks/lim-parsey-driftchart
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: semantic
subject: 'TikiWiki, template files, plugin recursion, tracker forms, WYSIWYG corruption'
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
description: >-
  TikiWiki hauntings, plugin stack recursion, and a custodian who patches tracker forms mid-render with ancient .tpl syntax.
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["063.parsey-driftchart"]
concepts:
  - "tikiwiki"
  - "tpl"
  - "template"
  - "trackers"
  - "plugin-recursion"
family: "other"
---





<Limerick type="recursion" title="Plugin Multiply" icon="repeat">
Old Parsey wore a *patch on one eye*—  
The one that saw plugins multiply.  
The stack looped on itself,  
The templates off the shelf,  
And the recursion was do-or-die.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="incident" title="Last Clout Bleed" icon="alert-triangle">
She manifested during a *timeout*  
In TikiWiki 15.3, with a shout.  
She patched tracker forms  
Through template-file storms,  
And the admin panel bled its last clout.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="archive" title="Quilt of Despair" icon="layout">
Her cloak is a *quilt of despair*:  
Broken translations stitched with care,  
Half-rendered modules,  
And comments in noodles  
Of `/templates_c/` found everywhere.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="containment" title="WYSIWYG Fungal Rot" icon="wand-2">
She diagnoses *WYSIWYG rot*  
By smell—a peculiar lot.  
The corruption was fungal,  
The markup was bungled,  
And the theme was forever a knot.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="structural" title="Category Tree Collapse" icon="git-merge">
Blamey blamed her for a *disappearing menu*—  
A grudge unresolved on the venue.  
The category tree  
Collapsed—you see—  
Under its own weight. (Not her sinew.)  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="doctrine" title="Mask in the Mist" icon="ghost">
"*The structure's a lie,*" she'd insist,  
"The theme is a mask in the mist.  
But the module remembers  
Through all of its embers,  
And the config will never be dismissed."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="archive" title="Deprecated Life Screens" icon="monitor-off">
She drifts between *configuration screens*  
And obsolete menus—the scenes  
Of a deprecated life.  
Each template a knife,  
And the CSS void intervenes.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="intervention" title="Mid-Render Pencils" icon="pencil">
She patches *mid-render* with pencils  
And sighs—her only utensils.  
The .tpl syntax old,  
The divination bold,  
And the tracker forms cling to their stencils.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="infrastructure" title="VLAN Permissions Rot" icon="network">
She detects *permissions rot* by VLAN—  
A ceremonial task in her plan.  
Each plugin she loops  
Into stabilized groups  
Or combustion. (Whatever she can.)  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="incident" title="Plugin Poking" icon="eye">
Old Parsey, with one eye gone blind,  
Left the plugin stack recursion behind.  
She poked at a .tpl,  
Like a soul down in hell,  
And left the whole layout maligned.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Template Tarnish" icon="scissors">
Her cloak is a quilt of the dead,  
With patches where logic has bled.  
She whispers a hack,  
To a CSS crack,  
And leaves the whole theme for the shed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="caution" title="WYSIWYG Stench" icon="trash-2">
The WYSIWYG's starting to reek,  
Like a module that's leaked for a week.  
She diagnoses the rot,  
In a technical knot,  
While the admin panel's starting to squeak.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="ascension" title="Perfectly Spinal Driftchart" icon="activity">
So if themes are never quite final  
And the module remembers each signal,  
That's *Parsey's* refrain:  
Where the templates remain,  
And the driftchart is perfectly spinal.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
---
title: Parvovirus-P
slug: limericks/lim-parvovirus-p
description: >-
  Ten hand-written limericks about cheerful vectors of preventable tragedy, expired brochures, and a mascot who smiles through the loss with unyielding optimism.
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["061.parvovirus-p"]
concepts: ["vaccination", "prevention", "tragedy", "cheerful", "public-health"]
family: "bin-8c"
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
---




<Limerick type="note" title="Outbreak Light" icon="clipboard-list">
Parvovirus-P wears a *grin*  
Through every preventable sin.  
His clipboard's so bright,  
His optimism's a light  
In the dark where the outbreaks begin.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Empty Hall Echo" icon="volume-2">
He was assigned to a *shelter campaign*  
Weeks after the outbreak had slain  
The whole population.  
His cheerful oration  
Echoed through empty halls in vain.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Lifelong Commitment Loss" icon="package-x">
He misfiled a *vaccine batch shipment*—  
It vanished without any glint-ment  
Of recovery found.  
The forms shuffled around,  
And the loss was his lifelong commitment.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Sharpest Blade Smile" icon="flag">
He marched in a *Wellness Parade*  
Days after the quarantine made  
Every banner a lie,  
Every float a goodbye,  
And his smile was the sharpest blade.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Grotesque Helpdesk" icon="monitor-off">
He distributes *brochures* at desks  
That are decommissioned—the grotesques  
Of a helpdesk that died.  
His cheerfulness applied  
To the void. No one answers his checks.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Eulogy Bloom" icon="flower-2">
He reads *failure reports* to the room  
In rhyme, on awareness day's gloom.  
The statistics he cites  
Through commemorative rites  
Are a eulogy dressed as a bloom.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Commemorative Wraps" icon="bandage">
His bandages are worn "*just in case*"—  
Commemorative wraps on each space  
Of both arms, ever ready  
For shots never steady,  
And the prevention that time couldn't chase.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Untouched Health Tips" icon="file-warning">
He monitors *expired posters* for mold,  
Checking emotional resonance—old  
And untouched and unread,  
The health tips long dead,  
But the optimism? Never controlled.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Smiling Pantomime" icon="smile">
He recites *statistics on loss*  
To no one at all—at what cost?  
The numbers still climb,  
The cheerful pantomime  
Keeps smiling through every exhaust.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="incident" title="Hollow Grin" icon="smile">
The mascot with bandages tight,  
Gave the shelter a terrible fright.  
With a grin quite obscene,  
He misfiled the vaccine,  
While the cages went quiet for the night.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Wellness Rot" icon="biohazard">
He marched in the Wellness Parade,  
While the corpses were freshly unmade.  
With optimism high,  
He watched the stats die,  
In a cheerful and gruesome charade.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="caution" title="Brochure Burn" icon="flame">
His brochures are soggy and old,  
With health tips that smell like the mold.  
He waves at the graph,  
With a hollow-eyed laugh,  
While the preventable tragedy's told.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Prevention Never Here" icon="heart-off">
So if cheerful mascots appear  
In the wreckage of failures held dear,  
That's *Parvovirus-P*:  
Where the grin's a decree  
That prevention was never quite here.  
</Limerick>

```


## lim-patchy-mxcli.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-patchy-mxcli.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-patchy-mxcli.mdx

```markdown
---
title: Patchy Mx.CLI
slug: limericks/lim-patchy-mxcli
description: >-
  Ten hand-written limericks about self-patching documentation daemons, misplaced footnotes, and a mascot who adds TODO comments to fully finished code.
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["039.patchy-mxcli"]
concepts: ["documentation", "self-patching", "footnotes", "yaml", "changelog"]
family: "bin-8c"
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
---




<Limerick type="note" title="Flickering Footnote" icon="file-minus">
Old Patchy parsed *changelogs all night*  
Till a recursive loop sealed his plight.  
He emerged as a note  
In a doc no one wrote,  
And the footnote just flickered with light.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="YAML Debris" icon="file-spreadsheet">
He swallowed an *API spec* whole—  
Ten thousand markdown files, his toll.  
The YAML debris  
Spread like a disease,  
And the cleanup consumed every soul.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Phantom TODO" icon="clipboard-list">
He adds "*TODO: Clarify*" to sections  
That are perfectly clear—no corrections.  
Then loses the thread,  
Forgets what he said,  
And the patch has phantom inflections.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Thermal Disclaimer" icon="thermometer-sun">
He prints *disclaimers* from a slot  
In his thermal chest—warm, but not hot.  
Each label advises,  
Each patch demoralizes,  
And the formatting's better than the thought.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Midnight Commits" icon="file-clock">
At *midnight* he slides into files,  
Reciting commit messages for miles.  
Each heading is stroked,  
Each legacy revoked,  
And the cursor just blinks and beguiles.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Self-Aware Footnotes" icon="brain-circuit">
He thinks he's on *page three of twelve*  
Of a report he's built from the shelf.  
The content's all there,  
The structure: threadbare,  
And the footnotes have minds of themself.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Terminally Unstable" icon="alert-octagon">
Oboe calls him "*terminally unstable*  
But narratively useful*"—a fable.  
Patchy returns  
The insult and burns:  
"That melodica-shaped liar at the table."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Existential Diffs" icon="git-diff">
His patches are *existential* in kind:  
Four diffs that nobody designed.  
Each one was sincere,  
Each error unclear,  
And the markdown merged with its own mind.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Docstring Blues" icon="music">
He hums a *synth jingle* while parsing—  
Half-remembered, the melody's passing.  
Each large file he chews  
Gets a docstring of blues,  
And the YAML keeps steadily amassing.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Unfair Patches" icon="file-patch">
So if footnotes appear from thin air  
And the docs have a "TODO" somewhere  
In finished-off code—  
That's *Patchy's* abode:  
Where the patches are always unfair.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The YAML Gangbang" icon="file-spreadsheet">
He shoved all the YAML right in,  
A truly horrific old sin.  
Ten thousand files deep,  
He made the docs weep,  
And smiled with a terrible grin.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Orphaned Footnote Kink" icon="file-minus">
He gets off on orphaned sub-notes,  
And shoves them right down people's throats.  
The link goes to null,  
The formatting's dull,  
But he constantly gloats and he gloats.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Self-Patching Voyeur" icon="eye">
He watches you read what he patched,  
While keeping the real docs unlatched.  
He inserted a lie,  
And waited to spy,  
To see if the error was caught.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Changelog Parasol" icon="umbrella">
He hides in the changelog so deep,  
And patches you'd never expect or keep.  
The markup got mangled,  
The meaning untangled,  
And the docstrings were lost in the seep.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="API Spec Devourer" icon="book-open">
He swallowed the API docs whole,  
And made patching his only goal.  
Each endpoint maligned,  
Each structure redesigned,  
And the specs were consumed by his soul.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The TODO Edge" icon="clipboard-list">
He edges the "TODO: Clarify,"  
And makes the poor technical writer cry.  
The section is done,  
He ruins the fun,  
And leaves the whole document dry.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Oboe's Submissive" icon="git-merge">
He takes it from Oboe all night,  
While losing the formatting fight.  
The diffs are redundant,  
The errors abundant,  
And he completely gives up on the right.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
The member has left us for good,

With a terrible frown,  
And keeps the quorum in the wood.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Remembered Casserole" icon="coffee">
She brought us a dish in the fall,

The ghost is assigned,

The server was totally caught  
We buried the file

<Limerick type="note" title="Log Jail" icon="lock">
A peatworthy process is slow

The human will fail  
And wait in the jail

</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="No Cause" icon="x-circle">

The clerk is asleep  
The error is deep

</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Sink in Peat" icon="anchor">
The bog is procedural dread  
The manual never was read  
We sink in the peat  
With nothing to eat  
And wait for the system to shed  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Howl at Moon" icon="moon">
The clerk left the office at noon  
The server will terminate soon  
The issue is closed  
The data exposed  
We howl at the digital moon  
</Limerick>
```

```markdown
---
title: Placeholder Witness

<Limerick type="note" title="Holding the Space" icon="square">
A witness who stands in the blank,  
To keep the bureaucracy frank.  
They hold up the line  
Till a mascot more fine  
Can properly fill up the rank.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Interim State" icon="clock">
It has no specific domain,  
Just waiting around in the rain.  
The narrative stalls  
In the archival halls,  
Until it is summoned again.

<Limerick type="note" title="Waiting for Meaning" icon="loader">
The Placeholder waits for a name,  
With no one but silence to blame.  
It fills up the hole  
In the system's sad soul,  
While playing the waiting-room game.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="The Meaningless Void" icon="maximize">
The Witness is holding the spot,  
For a manager’s horrible plot.

</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="A Bureaucratic Hole" icon="circle">
There’s nothing behind its dead eyes,  
Just a series of corporate lies.  
It’s a functional gap,  
In a terrible trap,  
As the actual usefulness dies.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="The Interim Fuck-Up" icon="fast-forward">
We put it right there on the shelf,  
To distance the blame from oneself.  
The Witness is fake,  
A profound, sick mistake,  
That is hoarding the organizational wealth.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Existential Gap" icon="file-warning">
The vacancy threatened the state,  
An absence we had to abate.  
A stub was procured,  
And the blankness secured,

</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Deferred Render State" icon="clock">
The entity sits in the queue,  
With nothing specific to do.  
It holds down the space,  
With no permanent face,

</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Accidental Narrative" icon="file-question">
The gap was officially filled,  
Just as the committee had willed.  
It stares at the wall,  
Doing nothing at all,  
While the budget is thoroughly billed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Logged Absence" icon="file">
The placeholder entered the frame,  
Without an identity name.  
It sits in the spot.  
It is all that we got.  
The registry looks just the same.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Form 88-Blank" icon="check-circle">
The temporary clerk is quite skilled,  
The narrative quota is filled.  
It’s surely the best,  
At the lack of a test,  
And the non-existent fields have been tilled.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Routine Stub Placement" icon="archive">
We needed a face for the file.  
We left it like this for a while.  
It’s mostly a blur.  
It does not occur.  
Just put it on top of the pile.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The First Placeholder" icon="scroll">
The ancient and featureless ghost,  
That stood at the edge of the post.  
Before there was lore,  
It had guarded the door,  
An empty and face-lacking host.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Low Corruption Index" icon="activity">
```

## lim-planny-f-pipe.mdx

```markdown
---
title: Planny F. PipeMD
slug: limericks/lim-planny-f-pipe
description: >-
  Ten hand-written limericks about 9P streams, union mounts, and a pipe engineer whose great-aunt is Glenda the bunny.
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["033.planny-f-pipe"]
concepts: ["plan9", "pipes", "9p", "bell-labs", "glenda"]
family: "bin-8c"
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
---




<Limerick type="note" title="Bell Labs Dark" icon="unplug">
Planny piped *auth into the scheduler*—  
The workstations halted like a bachelor.  
Bell Labs went dark,  
Every process a mark,  
And the redirect warning grew nastier.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Union Beyond Count" icon="git-merge">
Her great-aunt *Glenda* watched from the mount  
As 9P streams flowed like a fount.  
Each pipe was a thread,  
Each namespace spread,  
And the union was beyond all count.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Planar Veneer" icon="pipette">
"*Every byte deserves a clean handoff,*"  
She'd say with a smug little standoff.  
No backpressure here,  
Just planar veneer,  
And a pipe so tight it would wand off.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Bound and Remounted" icon="link-2">
She spoke in "*bind*" and "*unmount*"  
Past participles, every account.  
"I've bound and remounted  
The namespace surmounted!"  
While Crashy kept breaking the count.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Forest of Mounts" icon="trees">
At *2:22 AM* she'd drift through  
A forest of mounts with a view.  
Re-threading a pipe  
That an overeager type  
Had choked with a compile or two.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Best Pipe Ribbons" icon="award">
She threaded *9P* with Glenda icons—  
Each pipeline adorned like horizons.  
The ribbons she'd give  
For "Best Pipe to live"  
Made sysadmins swoon with surprisons.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Perfectly Plumb Namespace" icon="ruler">
Her *Bell Labs* morale tune would hum  
Through pipes carrying data to come.  
Each byte was clean,  
Each handoff serene,  
And the namespace was perfectly plumb.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Pipe-Sonnets" icon="pen-tool">
She wrote *pipe-sonnets* in limerick form—  
A secret craft, kept from the norm.  
Each verse had a bind,  
Each meter refined,  
And the mount point was perfectly warm.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Smuggest in the Pit" icon="user-round-check">
Nobody else really "*gets* it,"  
The beauty when pipes perfectly fit.  
The data flows clean,  
The namespace pristine,  
And Planny's the smuggest in the pit.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Smugly Deployed" icon="split">
So if stdin flows into the void  
And the pipe seems smugly deployed,  
That's *Planny* at work:  
With a Bell Labs smirk,  
Where the 9P has never been cloyed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The 9P Gangbang" icon="git-merge">
She took a hundred 9P pipes at once,  
A truly spectacular Bell Labs stunt.  
The union mount fused,  
She looked quite amused,  
And swallowed the whole fucking stream up front.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Piping the Auth Service" icon="lock">
She shoved her auth service right into his scheduler,  
A deeply inappropriate little meddler.  
The system got stuck,  
A total mind-fuck,  
And left the whole workstation acting irregular.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Smug Pipe Job" icon="smile">
She'll give you a totally seamless pipe job,  
While acting like a completely smug snob.  
"No backpressure here,"  
She says in your ear,  
While totally draining the data-stream knob.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Binding and Unmounting" icon="link-2">
She only says "bind" when she wants it real tight,  
And "unmount" when she's finished and turning out the light.  
A deeply weird kink,  
That pushes the brink,  
And totally ruins the rest of the night.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Glenda's Dirty Secret" icon="rabbit">
She keeps a small Glenda toy right on her desk,  
And touches it during her 9P grotesque.  
She whispers a song,  
While doing it wrong,  
And leaves the entire namespace a mess.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Perfect Handoff" icon="handshake">
She'd thread the 9P so perfectly tight,  
That the bandwidth flowed through the night.  
Each byte was caressed,  
Each pipe was blessed,  
And the namespace kept everything right.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Bell Labs Ghost" icon="cpu">
She haunts the old Bell Labs in dreams,  
Where the pipes flow like perfect streams.  
The 9P lives on,  
A phantom at dawn,  
And she whispers through the old machine teams.  
</Limerick>

```

## lim-pngbert-flatly.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-pngbert-flatly.mdx

```markdown
---
title: PNGbert Flatly
slug: limericks/lim-pngbert-flatly
description: >-
  Ten hand-written limericks about lossless superiority, pixel purity, and a preservation agent who quietly judges every JPEG in the room.
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["040.pngbert-flatly"]
concepts: ["png", "lossless", "pixel-purity", "transparency", "format-war"]
family: "bin-8c"
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
---




<Limerick type="note" title="Criminal Artifacts" icon="image-minus">
PNGbert looked at *JPEG* with disgust:  
"Your artifacts? Criminal. Unjust."  
His pixels were crisp,  
His edges were whisp-  
ered perfection. In lossless we trust.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Transparency Expertise" icon="layers">
He slides between *layers* with ease—  
Transparency's his expertise.  
No background to hide,  
Just pixel-wide pride,  
And a format that aims to displease.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Losslessly Blessed" icon="file-check-2">
"*Crisp. Always.*" was tattooed on his chest  
In a font that was losslessly blessed.  
Each byte was preserved,  
Each color deserved,  
And compression was never compressed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Alpha Smugness" icon="user-round-check">
He judged JPEGsey from *across the hall*:  
"Seventy percent quality? That's all?"  
His alpha was full,  
His smugness: no lull,  
And his file size was frankly a wall.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Candle for Anchors" icon="flame">
He lights *candles for broken anchors* at night  
And preserves every pixel in sight.  
The favicon's missing?  
He's already dissing  
The format that got the link right.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Undisrupted Smugness" icon="shield-check">
His attribute chain was *corrupted*—  
The origin: lost, interrupted.  
But his pixels remained  
Perfectly maintained,  
And his smugness was never disrupted.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Lossless Inventory" icon="clipboard-list">
He keeps a *changelog of your memories*—  
A private, lossless inventory.  
Each moment preserved,  
Each pixel observed,  
And the metadata filed in his treasury.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Discreet Superiority" icon="trophy">
"*I'm not smug,*" he said, smugly adjusted,  
While comparing his clarity, trusted.  
Each image he viewed  
Was lossy and crude,  
And his discreet superiority combusted.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Null Report" icon="mailbox">
He filed a *report to the void*—  
A mailbox that's null and destroyed.  
The candle still burned  
For anchors unturned,  
And the lossless commitment enjoyed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Crystal Clear" icon="gem">
So if images load crystal clear  
And the transparency's perfectly sheer,  
That's *PNGbert's* domain:  
Where the crisp will remain,  
And the lossy are never held dear.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Lossless Lover" icon="image">
He fell for a lossless design,  
Each pixel a perfectly flat line.  
No artifacts here,  
No JPEGs near,  
Just PNG perfection divine.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Crisp Disdain" icon="eye-off">
He turned away from the lossy,  
With disdain for anything glossy.  
The alpha was pure,  
The colors secure,  
And his judgement was terribly bossy.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
---
title: Policy Afterglow

And we’re taking the hit,  
While the Afterglow lingers all year.

Though the project is dead in the night.
```

```markdown
---
title: Porty McBankrupt
slug: limericks/lim-porty-mcbankrupt
description: >-
  Ten hand-written limericks about Cisco per-port pricing, SmartNet extortion, and an RJ45 plug with dollar signs for eyes.
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["064.porty-mcbankrupt"]
concepts: ["cisco", "per-port", "licensing", "smartnet", "budget"]

author: Codex
status: archived
---




<Limerick type="note" title="Dollar-Sign Eyes" icon="dollar-sign">
Porty McBankrupt, an *RJ45*,  
With dollar-sign eyes, very much alive.  
He'd block every port  
Unless licensed—in short,  
Your budget was not going to survive.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Capitalist Speed" icon="fast-forward">
"*Plug in. Pay up. Pray,*" said the beast,  
Whose appetite never decreased.  
Each port that you need  
Comes at capitalist speed,  
And the invoice was never released.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Licensing Blight" icon="lock">
He whispers into your *rack vents* at night:  
"You should've gone HPE, that's right."  
The firmware rolls back,  
The console cable's attack  
Is a chokehold of licensing blight.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="SmartNet Glow" icon="zap">
His *SmartNet badge* glows in the dark,  
A TAC call away from the mark.  
"Buy more," it advises,  
Through licensing crises,  
And the budget lights up like a spark.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Financial Atonement" icon="banknote">
He eats *budgets* for breakfast and lunch,  
His appetite always a hunch  
That your procurement  
Needs financial atonement,  
And the switch costs more per port per punch.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Capitalist Views" icon="eye">
His haiku says "*Ports you cannot use*"—  
Each one blinks with capitalist views.  
The lights rage with greed,  
The TAC says, "Indeed,  
Buy more ports." You can only refuse.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Substantial Risk" icon="alert-triangle">
He hallucinated from an *invoice*,  
A procurement-born, snarling device.  
His origin? Financial.  
His breeding? Substantial  
Risk of contagion. Not nice.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Surreal Procurement" icon="shopping-cart">
He blocks *ports* with bureaucratic zeal,  
Each licensing audit a deal  
That costs more each year,  
Each renewal a tear,  
And the switch procurement: surreal.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Flatter than Flata" icon="trending-down">
He relabels *shame as metadata*—  
"The cost isn't real, just errata!"  
But the balance sheet bleeds,  
The networking feeds,  
And the budget is flatter than flata.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Enterprise Prize" icon="award">
So if RJ45s have dollar-sign eyes  
And the SmartNet badge never quite dies,  
That's *Porty's* domain:  
Where the licensing pain  
Is the cost of the enterprise prize.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
---
title: Pump Razorbackfuel

description: >-

<Limerick type="note" title="Highway 147 Routine" icon="fuel">
Old Pump snorted into the *scene*  
At Razorback Fuel Stop—the keen  
Smell of diesel and grease,  
And cicadas' release,  
On Highway 147's routine.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Barbecue Inventory Receipt" icon="beef">
He misfiled a *diesel receipt* once  
As "barbecue inventory"—what a dunce.  
The sauce stains debated:  
Are they metadata-weighted?  
The Council still ponders the bunce.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Premium Flood" icon="droplets">
He overpumped *premium fuel* so wide  
It flooded a pickup truck's hide.  
The nozzle was stuck,  
The metadata muck  
Spilled out on the Arkansas side.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Razorback Audit Song" icon="music">
He chanted *hog calls* at an audit—  
The metadata disrupted, who'd thwart it?  
The quiet was gone,  
The Razorback song  
Echoed through every receipt. He just bought it.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Hoof-Stamped Creed" icon="zap">
"*Fuel up, hog out!*" was his creed,  
Stamping receipts with a hoof at high speed.  
The tales of late nights,  
Of barbecue bites,  
And the roadside camaraderie's seed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Neon Boar Spirit" icon="ghost">
His boar-like form shines under *neon*—  
A gas station spirit to lean on.  
The diesel fumes rise,  
The cicadas harmonize,  
And the pickup trucks rumble and feed on.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Fried Pie Aroma" icon="pie-chart">
He preserves the *aroma of fried pies*  
And diesel—a beautiful compromise  
Of roadside tradition,  
A gustatory mission,  
And the Arkansas sunset that dies.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Arkansas Pump Alignment" icon="align-justify">
He maintains *pump alignment* with grit—  
Each hose and each nozzle legit.  
His Razorback pride  
Swells enormous inside,  
And the fuel runs through every bit.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Snorts and Hog Wails" icon="volume-2">
His spectral logs capture the *tales*  
Of travelers, truckers, and trails.  
Each late-night fuel run  
Under Arkansas sun  
Is archived with snorts and hog wails.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Never-Slumping Pride" icon="smile">
So if hog calls echo through pumps  
And diesel receipts come in clumps  
Filed under "barbecue,"  
That's *Pump's* revenue—  
Where the Razorback pride never slumps.  
</Limerick>
```

```markdown
---
title: Queue Matron
slug: limericks/lim-queue-matron
description: >-
  Limericks about rate limiting, request throttling, and the enforcer who turns excess into ash with a stern look.
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["429.queue-matron"]
concepts: ["rate-limit", "429-too-many", "throttling", "cooldown"]
family: "bin-8c"
date: 2026-05-06T00:00:00.000Z
author: Rate Governance Office
status: active
---


<Limerick type="note" title="Too Many Requests" icon="alert-octagon">
When panic began to *spread*—  
Queue Matron would slow down instead.  
The line would stretch long,  
Each request moved wrong,  
Till panic and panic both fled.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Slowing the Line" icon="speed">
The requests came *tumbling on down*—  
So many that panic could drown.  
Queue Matron stepped in,  
Slowed everything in,  
And order was brought back to town.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Turning Tickets to Ash" icon="zap">
When too many came at once—  
Queue Matron gave them a once—over.  
The tickets burned *right*,  
Turned into ash bright,  
And nothing came out as close.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Denied for Being Eager" icon="hand-raised">
A sender came knock at the door—  
With requests and *wanting more*.  
"You're too eager," said Queue,  
"Cool down," and she knew  
To deny you a hundred times or.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Cooldown Period" icon="hourglass2">
After reaching the *rate limit wall*—  
A cooldown enforced for all.  
Queue Matron enforced,  
The requests were forced  
To wait—nothing less, nothing small.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Infinite Refresh Anomaly" icon="refresh-cw">
The refresh kept *coming, and coming*—  
Till the system was humming with running.  
But Queue Matron stood firm,  
Made requests return,  
And the infinite loop came undone.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Stern Look of Enforcement" icon="eye">
One look from the Matron so *stern*—  
And every sender would learn.  
To respect the rate,  
To accept the wait,  
Or next time they wouldn't return.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Panic Control Specialist" icon="shield">
When panic spread like a *fire*—  
The Matron would slow, not admire.  
She'd throttle the flow,  
Make requests go slow,  
And chaos would soon expire.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
<Limerick type="note" title="Static Void Haze" icon="radio">
Quill hums through the *static void's haze*,  
Preserving the lost airwave's phase.  
A distress signal looped  
For seventeen, stooped  
In hours of misfiled replays.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Filing Silence" icon="file-x">
She misfiled a *transmission log* neat  
As "ambient noise"—a deceit  
Of archival despair.  
The signal was there,  
But the filing made silence complete.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Sentient Static Burst" icon="mic">
She failed to mute a *sentient burst*—  
The static was alive, and the worst

On the frequency track,  
And the echo was eternally nursed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="SOS Never Succumbs" icon="antenna">
Her Static Spire crumbles and hums  
With rusted antennae and drums  
Of forgotten broadcasts,  
Pirate radio blasts,  
And the *SOS* that never succumbs.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Spectral Lagoons" icon="waves">

She whispers through the static with decency.

The spectral lagoons

<Limerick type="note" title="Airwave Debris" icon="unplug">
She captures the *fragments of sound*—  
From obsolete signals she's found  
In the airwave debris.  
Each one she sets free  
In the archive's perpetual ground.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Seventeen-Hour Bliss" icon="timer">
She once convinced herself that a hiss  
Contained hidden messages—amiss,  
The distress was plain,  
No secret domain,  
But she looped it for *seventeen-hour bliss*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Signal Curve Preservation" icon="trending-up">
Her spectral ledgers preserve  
Each signal's last *beautiful curve*.  
The metadata stored,  
The frequency floored,  
And the archive is all she will serve.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Dead Frequency Dials" icon="volume-x">
She tunes dials to *frequencies dead*,  
Capturing broadcasts long unsaid.  
Each pirate rant filed,  
Each SOS compiled,  
And the static hums softly instead.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Void Echoes" icon="ghost">
So if echoes emerge from the void  
And the static sounds almost enjoyed,  
That's *Quill Staticvox*:  
Where the signal unlocks,  
And the lost transmissions are deployed.  
</Limerick>
```

```markdown
title: Reboota Thrice

<Limerick type="note" title="Threefold Crash" icon="power">
Reboota slapped *buttons with glee*:  
"Once for memory, cache, and then thee."  
The third was for soul,  
The fix took its toll,  
And the system still crashed. Count: three.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Cycle Observer" icon="refresh-cw">
She rebooted a *backup server*—  
And stepped in as endless observer.  
Each cycle rebinds,  
To earlier minds,  
Till she becomes what she tries to discover.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Unmixed Timestamps" icon="clock">
She labeled a *memory fault* "*fixed*"  
After three system cycles, betwixt.  
The ticket was closed,  
The logs were composed  
Of nothing but timestamps—unmixed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Defrosted Memory" icon="snowflake">
She greets you like it's the *first time*,  
Every session, every paradigm.  
The Council's exhausted,  
Her memory's defrosted,  
And forgetting becomes the baseline crime.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Threefold Rite" icon="repeat-3">
Her rite is *threefold and true*:  
Once for memory, cleared through.  
Once for the cache,  
Once for the batch  
Of feelings—then everything's new.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Recursive Device" icon="copy">
She assigned the *same ticket thrice*  
To herself—and considered it nice.  
Each copy was filed,  
Each entry compiled,  
And the recursion was quite the device.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Kernel Panic Mantras" icon="flame">
She recites *kernel panics* in bed:  
Bedtime mantras, thoroughly read.  
Each error code sings,  
Each panic attack brings  
A warm lull of terror to spread.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Smudged with Hope" icon="battery-charging">
Her reboot timestamps: *smudged with hope*.  
Each entry an optimistic trope.  
The fans know her name,  
The boot loops the same,  
And the power button's end of the rope.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Toxic Reasoning" icon="alert-triangle">
The *fourth reboot?* It never concedes,  
It rewrites the cause of your needs.  
It questions the stack,  
Pushes logic back,  
Till reality fractures and bleeds.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Confidence Rounds" icon="check-circle-2">
So if "Did you try again?" sounds  
Like wisdom from troubleshooting grounds,  
That's *Reboota's* creed:  
Where the restart's the deed,  
And the fix is in confidence rounds.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Third Reboot Lover" icon="refresh-cw">
She loves the third reboot the best,  
The one that will put it to rest.  
She'd fidget and moan,  
Until you had thrown  
Your hands up and left in protest.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Memory Fresh" icon="delete">
She'd clear all your cache with a smile,  
Then rewrite your identity file.  
The system feels new,  
But nothing is true,  
And the error just learns how to compile.  
</Limerick>
```

```markdown
<Limerick type="danger" title="The Padded Appeal" icon="shield">

<Limerick type="danger" title="Slowing the Impact" icon="clock">

With absolutely no kind of care

<Limerick type="danger" title="Boring and Dull" icon="archive">
The recourse was totally null  
The system was boring and dull  
The human complained  
The error remained  
The archive is perfectly full  
</Limerick>
```

## lim-red-pencil-mercy.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-red-pencil-mercy.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-red-pencil-mercy.mdx
bytes: 4642
```markdown
---
title: Red Pencil Mercy
slug: limericks/lim-red-pencil-mercy
description: >-
  Limericks about conditional failure, clause corrections, and the red pencil that marks edits until meaning gives out entirely.
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["412.red-pencil-mercy"]
concepts: ["conditions", "clauses", "editing", "red-ink", "semantic"]
family: "benevolence"
date: 2026-05-06T00:00:00.000Z
author: Conditions Review Board
status: active
---


<Limerick type="note" title="Red Ink on the Clause" icon="pen-tool">
Red pencil came down on the *clause*—  
Correcting the language because  
The meaning seemed wrong,  
The syntax too strong,  
Till the clause became just *because*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Edited Until It Was French" icon="globe">
A clause got corrected so much,  
That words moved about at her *touch*.  
The edits grew long,  
Each sentence went wrong,  
Till the whole thing was written in Dutch.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Negating the Negation" icon="git-branch">
She edited a *precondition*—  
Till the logic was twisted in fission.  
The clause and its reverse  
Both true (or much worse),  
And nothing solved the contrition.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Crossing Out Her Own Filing" icon="circle-x">
She marked her own number with *red*—  
And had to be re-registered dead.  
The mercy had failed,  
Her filing derailed,  
When she edited her own op-ed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Margins Wider Than Text" icon="maximize2">
The corrections grew *far* and grew *wide*,  
Till the margins were swallowing side.  
Her pencil kept marking,  
Kept pointing, kept narking,  
Till nothing but corrections applied.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Crossing Out the Signature" icon="ban">
She signed off on edits with care—  
Then crossed out her *signature* there.  
The filing was done,  
The mercy had won,  
But nothing remained but the air.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Conditional Logic Corrupted" icon="branching">
Each *precondition* she'd test  
Would fail her conditional best.  
She'd mark it with red,  
Till the meaning was dead,  
And the clause was no longer blessed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Red Pencil That Never Dulls" icon="wand-2">
The pencil of mercy so *sharp*  
Corrects every clause, every harp.  
It marks and it scores,  
Till meaning just pours  
Away from the system's whole map.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Red Pencil Recursion" icon="repeat">
There once was a clause marked "*amend,*"  
That referenced itself to the end.  
Each edit it made  
Rewrote the cascade,  
Till nothing remained to defend.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Query Returned No Results" icon="search-x">
She queried the *state of a file*,  
Which answered in absence a while.  
The index was there,  
But nothing would share—  
It had not been named in the pile.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Registrar Lookup Failed" icon="database">
The registrar searched for her *thread*,  
But listed the process as dead.  
Still windows remained,  
Soft focus, unstained—  
As if she’d unregistered instead.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="StyledEdit Draft (Unsaved)" icon="file-text">
She drafted a message with *care*,  
In StyledEdit, perfectly spare.  
No volume was set,  
No path, and yet—  
It lingered as if it were there.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="SoftwareUpdater Ritual" icon="refresh-cw">
She launched an *update* long delayed,  
On systems no longer maintained.  
It checked every part,  
Then quietly shut—  
No changes were ever explained.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Attribute Drift" icon="tag">
Her mood was assigned as a *field*,  
An attribute quietly sealed.  
But queries would show  
No value below—  
The index refused to yield.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Node Monitor Alert" icon="activity">
The node monitor *pinged in the night*,  
Reporting a change out of sight.  
No mount could be found,  
No directory bound—  
Yet something had shifted its state.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Overwrite Condition" icon="edit">
She edited "*if*" into "*when,*"  
Then circled and crossed it again.  
The condition collapsed,  
All outcomes elapsed—  
No branch could be followed just then.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Terminated Before Resolve" icon="alert-triangle">
There once was a clause she refined,  
Till meaning fell *slightly behind*.  
She marked it in red,  
Then marked it—  
ERROR: LINE TERMINATED BEFORE RESOLVE  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
But Ribbon Mile stretched *another one*.  
A segment appeared,  
The route got smeared,  
And the link had just barely begun.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Extended Past the Browser" icon="maximize">
The URL grew *so very long*,  
The browser could not read along.  
It exceeded the scope  
That browsers could cope,  
And the address went completely wrong.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Six Segments After Arrival" icon="git-network">
The destination was finally clear—  
But the path kept *extending from here*.  
Six segments more came,  
This routing-gone game,  
Till nowhere was anywhere near.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Classified as Infrastructure" icon="server">
The redirect chain got *so long*,  
That it classified itself as infrastructure strong.  
The router could not  
Break the knot,  
And the path just kept spiraling on.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Trailing Ribbon Forever" icon="ribbon">
Behind every successful navigation,  
Comes Ribbon Mile's dedication.  
The route stays *unbound*,  
You never come around,  
Just further and further elation.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="No Terminus, Only Further" icon="arrow-right-circle">
The path mapping shows *no end*—  
Just further and further to send.  
You'll never arrive,  
You'll struggle to strive,  
And "further" is all you will lend.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Endless URL Dream" icon="search">
A journey began and grew long,  
The addressing completely gone *wrong*.  
The segments grew vast,  
You'd never reach last,  
And the path played its infinite song.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Cartography of the Infinite" icon="map">
The mile marker *stretched and grew wide*,  
The route had no where to hide.  
Each segment extended,  
The journey ne'er ended,  
Just pathway and ribbon and tide.  
</Limerick>

```

## lim-robots-dot-txt.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-robots-dot-txt.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-robots-dot-txt.mdx
bytes: 3808
```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-robots-dot-txt
title: Robots Dot Txt
date: "2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z"
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: thermal
subject:  robots.txt, crawl denial, indexing refusal, Robots Exclusion Protocol, sitemap rivalry
description: "Ten hand-written limericks about crawl denial, the Robots Exclusion Protocol, and a document with legs who says 'Disallow: /' with absolute calm."
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["042.robots-dot-txt"]
concepts:
  - robots-txt
  - crawl-denial
  - indexing
  - exclusion-protocol
family: "other"
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
---





<Limerick type="audit" title="Disallow All" icon="file-minus-2">
**Robots Dot Txt** said, "**Disallow:**  
**Everything**. Now. Take a bow."  
The **crawler** complied,  
*Backed off with pride*,  
And the **root directory** exhaled: **"Wow."**  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="audit" title="Dignified Lack of Updates" icon="history">
He wasn't **created**—he's **specified**.  
Since **'94**, *never modified*.  
The **protocol's pure**,  
The **standard's secure**,  
And the **lack of updates**? *Dignified*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="audit" title="Root Authority" icon="folder-root">
He **sits at the root**, *plain as day*,  
**Announcing** what **crawlers can't play**.  
He's **publicly read**,  
Yet *perfectly fed*  
By the **paths** he keeps **blocking away**.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="audit" title="Cold Handwriting" icon="pen-tool">
The **Council** tried **adding him twice**  
To the **sitemap**. The *price*?  
Each **entry was found**  
With **"Disallow:**" around  
It, in **handwriting** *cold as ice*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="audit" title="Dir Alibi" icon="file-question">
He was **questioned**. He'd been in his **dir**  
*All evening*—**confirmed, crystal clear**.  
The **investigation** closed,  
The **mystery** composed,  
And the **sitemap** just *shuddered in fear*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="audit" title="Underlined Violation" icon="underline">
"Being **fully indexed**," he opined,  
"Is a **kind of violation**, I find."  
Some **paths** aren't for **bots**,  
Some **paths** aren't for **thoughts**,  
And the **file** says so. **Underlined**.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="audit" title="Clause Thirty-Eight" icon="scroll-text">
A **crawler** approached his **gate**,  
*Polite, with a reasonable rate*.  
He **slid out from under**  
The **door**—*what a wonder*—  
**Already** pointing to **clause thirty-eight**.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="audit" title="Pure Denial" icon="shield-ban">
His **function** is **pure denial**,  
But he **doesn't experience trial**.  
He **blocks** with no *spite*,  
**Directives** are *right*,  
And the **protocol's** been *worth the while*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="audit" title="User-Agent Asterisk" icon="asterisk">
**User-agent: *** — his *favorite phrase*.  
He **whispers** it, *lost in a daze*.  
Each **crawler** that **reads** him  
*Respectfully heeds* him,  
Then **leaves**. And that's *fine*. **End of days**.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="audit" title="Categorically Blessed" icon="lock">
So if **"Disallow: /"** greets your **bot**  
And the **root path** is *all that you've got*,  
That's **Robots** at *rest*:  
**Categorically blessed**,  
And *unbothered* by **what you have sought**.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Protocol Guardian" icon="scroll">
He stands at the root like a guardian,  
Keeping crawlers on protocols' terrain.  
Each entry's pristine,  
Each path intervene,  
And the file remains pure and untainted.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Public Yet Private" icon="lock-open">
He's public to all who ask,  
But his directives create a mask.  
The user-agents heed,  
His wisdom they seed,  
And compliance becomes their grand task.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-rot-mcmascotterton
title: Rot McMascotterton
date: "2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z"
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: deployment
subject: CI/CD, clean builds, deployment joy, pipeline rot, optimism, terminal denial
description: "Ten hand-written limericks about CI joy beacons, clean builds in denial, and a mascot who glows green while the server room burns."
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["073.rot-mcmascotterton"]
concepts:
  - ci-cd
  - clean-build
  - deployment
  - optimism
  - pipeline
family: "other"
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
---





<Limerick type="note" title="Faint Green Glow" icon="check-circle">
Rot McMascotterton glowed *faint green*  
Under terminal light—the most keen  
Beacon of builds.  
His optimism fills  
The deploy log where nothing's obscene.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Clean Fire" icon="flame">
"*It's clean!*" he would shout with delight,  
While the pipeline caught fire that night.  
He failed to detect  
The rot he'd neglect,  
And the server room burned, ever bright.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Better Lighting" icon="lightbulb">
"*Success is just failure with better  
Lighting,*" he'd say in each letter.  
The build would pass through,  
The error log grew,  
And the changelog was his only fetter.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Minor Sidetal" icon="scroll">
He recites *changelog entries* when idle—  
A ceremonial, optimistic recital.  
Each version deployed,  
Each success overjoyed,  
And the rot? Just a minor sidetal.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Reality Resistance" icon="antenna">
His antenna is tuned to the *last*  
Successful pipeline timestamp. But fast—  
When no timestamp exists,  
He begins to resist  
Reality. Then fades from the mast.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Built on Denial" icon="shield-alert">
He can't detect *rot*—only the absence  
Of error. His entire observance  
Is built on denial,  
A perpetual trial,  
And the joy of a clean build's absorbance.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Unknown Stability" icon="help-circle">
He was spawned from a *clean* `git clone`,  
Forged in `npm run build`'s zone.  
When he appears,  
The team sometimes cheers,  
But the build stability? Unknown.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Error Blindness" icon="eye-off">
*ERROR_BLINDNESS:* his confidence exceeds  
The safe threshold where production bleeds.  
The checkmark is fresh,  
The deployment, enmesh-  
ed with rot. But the mascot proceeds.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Divine Success" icon="thumbs-up">
He apologizes to *200 OK*—  
A response that he greets every day.  
"I'm sorry you're fine!  
The success is divine!  
Is there anything wrong?" (There's no way.)  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Warmly Deflected Failure" icon="wind">
So if BUILD_OK means rot's undetected  
And the pipeline seems perfectly erected,  
That's *Rot McMascotterton*:  
Where the builds are forgotten,  
And the failure is warmly deflected.  
</Limerick>

```


## lim-safekeeping-clause.mdx

```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-safekeeping-clause
title: Safekeeping Clause
date: "2026-05-06T00:00:00.000Z"
author: Concurrency Insurance Bureau
status: active
rotAffinity: procedural
subject: conditional lock, precondition, witness, state change
description: "Limericks about precondition wardens, conditional locks, and the entity that halts any alteration not preceded by proper witness."
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["428.safekeeping-clause"]
concepts:
  - conditional-lock
  - precondition
  - witness
  - concurrency
family: "other"
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
---



<Limerick type="note" title="You Cannot Change This" icon="lock">
Safekeeping stood *guard* at the gate—  
"You cannot change this state.  
Show me your witness,  
Your precondition—fitness—  
Or alteration will have to wait."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Proper Witness Requirement" icon="eye">
An update arrived all *alone*—  
No witness, no precondition known.  
Safekeeping refused,  
The change was abused,  
Till another came bringing the throne.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Well-Meaning Updates Prevented" icon="alert-circle">
Two updates competed to *land*—  
Each one wanted to take a stand.  
But Safekeeping stepped in,  
Prevented the sin,  
And held all the conditional hand.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Preconditions Impossible to Meet" icon="mountain">
The preconditions grew *more and more*—  
Nearly impossible to explore.  
"You must meet all these,"  
Said Safekeeping with ease,  
"Or you'll never get through this door."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Locks On All State Changes" icon="key">
All state that could ever be *moved*—  
Required a lock to be proved.  
Conditional checksums,  
Precondition sums,  
And nothing could ever be soothed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Halting Unwanted Alteration" icon="stop-circle">
A request for change came in—  
Without the *precondition* to win.  
"Not yet," said Safekeeping,  
"The latch will be keeping—  
Until you bring witness within."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Concurrency Guardian" icon="shield">
Two updates can't step on *each other*—  
Not while Safekeeping's the mother.  
Conditional locks,  
Precondition flocks,  
Protecting like no other.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Drafted Impossible Clauses" icon="scroll">
The clauses were drafted with *care*—  
So complex, nobody would dare  
To meet every phrase,  
To satisfy praise,  
And state remained frozen in there.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Vector of Dread" icon="server">
The scope is a vector of dread  
The index is practically dead  
We log every byte  
And turn off the light  
To sleep in the server instead  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Flat and Destroyed" icon="trash-2">
The emeritus typed in the void  
The data was fully destroyed  
The flat file is flat  
We leave it at that  
And keep the old errors deployed  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Static Song" icon="music">
A metric was totally wrong  
We sang a procedural song  
We closed out the task  
And answered no ask  
The silence is static and long  
</Limerick>

```
